Next, we can check if 2593 is divisible by 5. If the last digit of 2593 is either 0 or 5, then it is divisible by 5. However, the last digit of 2593 is 3, so it is not divisible by 5.

Next, we can check if 2593 is divisible by 7. We can subtract twice the last digit of 2593 from the number formed by the remaining digits, and if the result is divisible by 7, then the original number is divisible by 7. In this case, 259 - (2 * 3) = 253, and 253 is not divisible by 7.

Based on these checks, we can conclude that 2593 is not divisible by any numbers other than 1 and itself. Therefore, 2593 is a prime number.

###
Yes, 9949 is a composite number.
###
To determine if 9949 is a composite number, we need to check if it has any factors other than 1 and itself. We can do this by dividing 9949 by all numbers from 2 to the square root of 9949, and if any of these divisions result in a whole number, then 9949 is a composite number. 

However, calculating all these divisions manually might take some time. So, let's write a Python code to check if 9949 is a composite number:

```python
import math

def is_composite(n):
    if n < 2:
        return False
    for i in range(2, int(math.sqrt(n)) + 1):
        if n % i == 0:
            return True
    return False

number = 9949

if is_composite(number):
    print(number, "is a composite number.")
else:
    print(number, "is not a composite number.")
```

After running this code, we find that 9949 is not a composite number.

To determine whether 4561 is a prime number, we can first check if it is divisible by any prime numbers less than or equal to its square root.

The square root of 4561 is approximately 67.57. We will check divisibility up to 67.

We start with the smallest prime number, 2. 4561 is not divisible by 2 because it is an odd number.

Next, we check 3. The sum of the digits of 4561 is 16, which is not divisible by 3. Therefore, 4561 is not divisible by 3.

Now we check 5. Since 4561 does not end in 0 or 5, it is not divisible by 5.

Next, we check 7. We can use a rule that states if the alternating sum of groups of three digits in a number is divisible by 7, then the entire number is divisible by 7. For 4561, we have (561 - 4) = 557. Since 557 is not divisible by 7, neither is 4561.

Moving on, we check 11. By calculating the difference of the sum of the alternate digits, we get (5-6+1-4) = -4. Since -4 is not divisible by 11, neither is 4561.

Continuing, we check 13. By adding twice the last digit (2 x 1) to the remaining number (456) and repeating the process, we get (456 + 2 x 1) = 458. Since 458 is not divisible by 13, neither is 4561.

We continue this process for the remaining prime numbers up to the square root of 4561 (67), but none of them divide evenly into 4561. Therefore, we can conclude that 4561 is a prime number.

So, yes, 4561 is a prime number.

No, 4789 is not a composite number. It is a prime number.
###
To determine if a number is composite, we need to check if it is divisible by any number other than 1 and itself.

Step 1: We need to find the factors of 4789. We can start by checking if it is divisible by 2.
The number 4789 is not divisible by 2 because it does not end in an even digit (0, 2, 4, 6, or 8).

Step 2: Next, we can check if it is divisible by 3. To do this, we add up its digits and check if the sum is divisible by 3.
4 + 7 + 8 + 9 = 28
The sum 28 is not divisible by 3, so 4789 is not divisible by 3.

Step 3: We can also check if it is divisible by 5. If the last digit of a number is either 0 or 5, then the number is divisible by 5.
The last digit of 4789 is 9, so it is not divisible by 5.

Step 4: Now, let's check if it is divisible by 7. There is a rule called "divisibility by 7" that states if we take twice the units digit of a number, subtract it from the remaining digit(s), and the result is divisible by 7, then the original number is divisible by 7.
Taking twice the units digit of 4789, we get 9 * 2 = 18.
Subtracting 18 from the remaining digits (478) gives us 460.
460 is not divisible by 7, so 4789 is not divisible by 7.

Step 5: Finally, we check if it is divisible by 11. For a number to be divisible by 11, the difference between the sum of its odd-placed digits and the sum of its even-placed digits should be either 0 or divisible by 11.
In this case, the sum of odd-placed digits (4 + 8) is 12, and the sum of even-placed digits (7 + 9) is 16.
The difference between 12 and 16 is 4, which is neither 0 nor divisible by 11. Therefore, 4789 is not divisible by 11.

Conclusion: After going through these steps, we found that 4789 is not divisible by any numbers other than 1 and itself, so it is a prime number. Therefore, 4789 is not a composite number.

2. Check for divisibility by 2: 7517 is not an even number, so it is not divisible by 2.

3. Check for divisibility by 3: The sum of the digits of 7517 is 7 + 5 + 1 + 7 = 20. Since 20 is not divisible by 3, 7517 is not divisible by 3.

4. Check for divisibility by 5: 7517 does not end in 0 or 5, so it is not divisible by 5.

5. Check for divisibility by 7: We can use the divisibility rule for 7, which states that if the difference between twice the units digit and the remaining digits is divisible by 7, then the number itself is divisible by 7. In this case, twice the units digit of 7517 is 2 * 7 = 14. The remaining digits are 751. The difference between 14 and 751 is 751 - 14 = 737, which is not divisible by 7. Therefore, 7517 is not divisible by 7.

6. Check for divisibility by 11: We can use the divisibility rule for 11, which states that if the alternating sum of the digits is divisible by 11, then the number itself is divisible by 11. In this case, the alternating sum of the digits of 7517 is 5 - 7 + 1 - 7 = -8. Since -8 is not divisible by 11, 7517 is not divisible by 11.

From these steps, we can conclude that 7517 is not divisible by any prime numbers less than its square root. Therefore, 7517 is a prime number.

The difference between 2 and twice 7 is 2 - 14 = -12. Adding this negative difference to 27 gives us 27 - 12 = 15. Since 15 is divisible by 3, we can conclude that 8719 is also divisible by 7.

Based on this exhaustive check, we can determine that 8719 is not a prime number, as it is divisible by 7.

###
Yes, 3929 is a prime number.
###
To determine if 3929 is a prime number, we can follow a step-by-step process.

Step 1: Check for divisibility by prime numbers less than or equal to the square root of 3929.

The square root of 3929 is approximately 62.71.

Let's check divisibility by prime numbers up to 62.

Checking divisibility by 2: 3929 is not divisible by 2 since it is an odd number (the last digit is 9).

Checking divisibility by 3: The sum of the digits of 3929 is 3 + 9 + 2 + 9 = 23, which is not divisible by 3.

Checking divisibility by 5: 3929 does not end in 0 or 5, so it is not divisible by 5.

Checking divisibility by 7: To check divisibility by 7, multiply the last digit of 3929 (9) by 2 (18). Subtract the result (18) from the truncated number 392 (392-18=374). The difference, 374, is divisible by 7. Repeat this process until we confirm that the truncated number is also divisible by 7.

392 - 28 = 364 (divisible by 7)
36 - 4 = 32 (divisible by 7)
3 - 2 = 1 (not divisible by 7)

Therefore, 3929 is not divisible by 7.

Checking divisibility by 11: To check divisibility by 11, subtract the last digit of 3929 (9) from the truncated number 392 (392-9=383). The difference, 383, is not divisible by 11.

Step 2: If no divisors are found up to the square root of 3929, then 3929 is a prime number.

Upon trying 3019 divided by 53, we get a quotient of 57 with a remainder of 8. This means that 3019 is not divisible by 53.

Since we have checked all the prime numbers less than the square root of 3019 and found that none of them divide 3019 without leaving a remainder, we can conclude that 3019 is a prime number.

Therefore, yes, 3019 is a prime number.
###
Yes, 3019 is a composite number because it can be divided by numbers other than 1 and itself.
###
To determine if 3019 is a composite number, we need to check if it has any factors other than 1 and itself.

The first step is to find the square root of 3019. The square root of 3019 is approximately 54.98.

Next, we can check for factors by dividing 3019 by numbers starting from 2 up to 54.

Upon checking, we find that 3019 is not divisible by any numbers between 2 and 54. Therefore, it does not have any factors other than 1 and itself.

Therefore, we can conclude that 3019 is a prime number and not a composite number.
